msg:The room is big and very clean. The sunshine is very good. Open the balcony to face the sun. It is very comfortable in the valley, with birds singing and flowers fragrant halfway up the mountain. The hot spring is just a 5-minute walk from the hotel. You can also get a shuttle bus at the door of the hotel. It can be reached in 2 minutes. There are 40 different hot springs. There is always one suitable for you. The red wine pool is fragrant and the medicinal spring is also great. There are also various children's entertainment projects inside the hotel, including slides, open-air swings, etc. You can also get small gifts when you check in. It is worth going back again and again. The price/performance ratio is very high. Even during the Spring Festival, you can avoid crowds and enjoy the hot springs. When I returned to the room, I was surprised to find the fruit provided by the hotel. It was a pleasant surprise.
